When the dislocation is in the lower part, gently handle the patient as described for those with hernias, and properly straighten the limb's joint; then place two tiles at the head and foot likewise; next insert the tile between the buttocks on the affected side near the form; ensure it is secured by damp cloths so that it does not slip from the patient, then extend each minister towards him, and the physician aligns them evenly with his hand to correct the dislocation.
S’elle revient, c’est boin.	 If it returns, it's good.
Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	 If not, place on a table and press as we have said for hernias, and handle the patient gently under the ribcage.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit; et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	And when the dislocation is before you, it must be hastily extended by hand, and according to what I have said; then place the mirror opposite the painful limb, and press with the other hand, extending down towards the groin.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches; et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table; et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz; adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve; et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus; et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors; puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	 If the dislocation is in place, it does not need to extend the patient's leg or lift off the ground but should be adjusted as if the hip were realigned initially with both hips; positioned on its face and the limb extended as previously stated, pressing onto the joint atop the table. When the patient extends their legs, they will be even; then place the buttocks, apply a bandage, and use one of the bindings so that the hip does not move; rest for three or four days, then release it, and place the cast underneath; if you see them are even, then tie again as before, leaving it for another three days. Then allow the patient to walk gently until the limb is fortified.
de la dislocation dou genoil	For dislocation of the knee joint
Li genous est desaluez selonc .iij. manieres: c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier; et ne desalue point devant.	The joint is dislocated in three ways: that is to say, forward and backward, and not sideways.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez; et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez; puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment; et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement; et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie; et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	 When the signs are such that you command the patient to bend his leg towards his hip, and if it does not reach its hip, know that it is dislocated; and in the restoration of all this, make the patient sit upright, extend his leg as much as he can, place your back against his face, and put your foot on his feet; then take hold of his thigh with your hands, retract between your thumbs, then bend both knees firmly; other aids are to extend his foot until the joint returns to its place, and the sign is that it lightly reaches its hip; apply a poultice afterward, straighten the leg against the hip for III or IV days, then release it; do not let the patient move about until the limb is comfortably settled.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	 And if the limb is not completely healed, provide strong treatment as we have said in the care of the hip, until it is sound.
de la dislocation dou talon	Regarding ankle dislocation
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The heels are at times numb, at times not fully dislocated, both inside and out.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee: li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	 And the signs are that the ankle is dislocated, try before reaching the part where it has been displaced: reductions should be gentle, and it must be stretched gently with hands as soon as possible when barely touched.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville; puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut; et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet; s’elle revient, c’est bien; se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient; et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide; puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet; puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent; puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	 And when it is completely displaced, one must make the patient sit upright directly, and insert the instrument along the leg above the ankle; then grasp the foot with your right hand, and then once again with your left twice, then extend upwards, and firmly place the foot upwards; do this twice as we have said, pulling and turning the foot. If it returns, that's good; if not, resume the operation, for it will return; and if it cannot return in this way, lay the patient on his back on the ground with a strap firmly placed between their thighs to prevent movement of the limb; then grasp one thigh and have others extend the foot towards them or its ligament that they hold onto at the neck of the foot. Then each assistant extends evenly, and the straps remain in place between the patient's thighcuits to keep still when stretching; then position mirrors symmetrically for the dislocation on their hands, and other assistants lift the healthy leg from below, and the dislocated part will return quickly.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois; puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain; puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors; et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	 When it reaches the desired point, apply the dressing and plug with wool on top, firmly wrap the bandage around the leg, and watch for nerves behind the ankle to ensure the ties are not too tight; then leave it for 2 or 3 days, and if the bandage softens, re-tighten the strain; then remove after another day or three days, and prevent the patient from walking for four days; and if they attempt before this period ends, it is not certain that they will not dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if an abscess occurs there, it is necessary to soothe it, as we have said elsewhere, until it is healthy again.
des dois	And of these two:
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	est les bene de la; and sof ;
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne; et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie; et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 If the dislocation is in any of the joints of your lower back or leg, you must have the patient sit upright or on a straight table, then place their foot under the joint and press firmly, until it returns; and when they are even, and nothing appears to be wrong, place II fingers under the sole of their foot, then bandage it firmly, and leave it for III days, then remove; and let them rest until healed.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	Of wound and dislocation together.
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert: si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis; et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit; et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne; et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis; et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples; et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	 When a wound comes with dislocation and it needs to be repaired, many times the patient dies: do not presume in its treatment unless you are knowledgeable about the art and have practiced it for long, and if you are compassabale and merciful and slow; do not act rashly. Start with calming measures on abscesses first, and let the patient entrust themselves to God's hand, if there is no hope of health; and when there is hope, mend the limb back into place so that the abscess may grow well; and once the limb is in place, administer soothing treatments on the abscess as needed, and tend to the wound appropriately with dried ointments; and if dislocation has caused fractures or small bones are broken, follow what I have said for simple ailments; and avoid going down the path of fear according to what I have said, because it will lead you astray from your duty and harm your body.
Amen	 Now comes to healing.
